// Soft Shadows

Texture2D<float4> t5 : register(t5);

Texture2D<float4> t1 : register(t1);

SamplerComparisonState s1_s : register(s1);

SamplerState s0_s : register(s0);

cbuffer cb0 : register(b0)
{
  float4 cb0[83];
}


Texture2D<float4> StereoParams : register(t125);

void main(
